 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 1.01 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>MICROSOFT CORPORATION </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>CONFLICT MINERALS
REPORT </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>FOR THE REPORTING PERIOD FROM </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>JANUARY&nbsp;1 TO DECEMBER&nbsp;31, 2015 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>I.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>INTRODUCTION </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">This Conflict Minerals Report (&#147;CMR&#148;) for MICROSOFT CORPORATION is presented to comply with Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">13p-1</FONT>
under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 (the &#147;Rule&#148;) for the reporting period from January&nbsp;1 to December&nbsp;31, 2015 (&#147;2015 reporting year&#148;). The report covers activities of all Microsoft majority-owned subsidiaries and
variable interest entities that are subject to the Rule (&#147;Microsoft&#148;). The Rule imposes certain due diligence and reporting obligations on US Securities and Exchange Commission (&#147;SEC&#148;) registrants whose manufactured products
(including products contracted to be made for each registrant) contain &#147;conflict minerals&#148; necessary to the functionality or production of those products. The Rule defines &#147;conflict minerals&#148; to include cassiterite,
columbite-tantalite, gold, wolframite and their derivatives limited to tin, tantalum, tungsten, and gold (collectively referred to as &#147;3TGs&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft develops and markets software, services, and hardware devices that deliver new opportunities, greater convenience, and enhanced value to
people&#146;s lives. Microsoft is committed to the responsible sourcing of raw materials globally in support of human rights, labor, health and safety, environmental protection, and business ethics. Our commitment and strategy are outlined in the
Microsoft <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Responsible Sourcing of Raw Materials</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> policy. Under our policy, Microsoft takes a holistic approach to responsible sourcing while working toward
the use of conflict-free minerals in our hardware devices (&#147;devices&#148;). One of our objectives is to ensure that we do not harm communities through an inadvertent <I>de facto</I> embargo of minerals from the Democratic Republic of the Congo
(&#147;DRC&#148;) or an adjoining country (defined as a country that shares an internationally recognized border with the DRC) - both considered a &#147;Covered Country&#148; for purposes of the Rule. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">This year&#146;s report documents our efforts for the 2015 reporting year, which demonstrate meaningful progress. The number of <FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Conflict-Free Smelter Program</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> (&#147;CFSP&#148;)-compliant smelters or refiners (the &#147;SORs&#148;) in
our supply chain increased from 148 to 213 due to targeted supplier outreach and maturation of the CFSP - of which Microsoft is a founding partner and strong supporter. Based on Microsoft&#146;s data analysis, we also concluded that 100 percent of
tantalum smelters identified in Microsoft&#146;s supply chain were CFSP compliant. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Since the 2014 reporting year (January 1 to
December&nbsp;31, 2014), we have also taken several notable actions to improve our conflict minerals due diligence, including the following: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Completed implementation of recommendations from third party audit firm covering 2014 reporting year external
assessment; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:26%">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> Please note: this CMR contains references and hyper-text links to non-Microsoft,
external websites. These links are provided for informational purposes only. Their inclusion in this CMR does not establish Microsoft&#146;s endorsement of or assumption of liability for content posted on these external websites. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">1 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Implemented process improvements to increase supplier response rate, including extensive sourcing manager involvement,
supplier resource support, and tailored outreach to both new suppliers and 2014 unresponsive suppliers; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Developed and refined internal controls and procedures to improve in-scope supplier determination, data collection and
validation, and supply chain due diligence, including early engagement with suppliers upon initial on-boarding through Microsoft&#146;s Social and Environmental Accountability (&#147;SEA&#148;) online Audit Management System; and
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Enhanced our supplier data collection process such as addition of automated &#147;red flags&#148; to identify quality
control issues and Covered Country sourcing risk early in the surveying process. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft devices contain one or more 3TGs and
are within the Rule&#146;s scope. Devices manufactured during the 2015 reporting year included: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Surface line of tablet and laptop computers and accessories; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Xbox gaming/entertainment consoles and accessories; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Personal computing accessories, including mice and keyboards; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Mobile devices, including Nokia and Lumia branded mobile phones and devices; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Surface Hub computing displays; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Microsoft Band wellness devices. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">On the basis of our performance of the required &#147;Reasonable Country of Origin Inquiry&#148; (&#147;RCOI&#148;) (see Section II), we cannot exclude
the possibility that some of the 3TGs contained in our devices may have originated in a Covered Country. Therefore, we are submitting this CMR, which describes the conflict minerals due diligence we performed, as an exhibit to our Form SD. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">We are submitting this CMR to the SEC under the reporting requirements of the Rule and have published the CMR externally on our corporate website: see <FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Responsible Sourcing</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">. The manufacture of devices during any specified time period may include raw materials sourced before, as well as during, that time period.
In particular, some 3TGs used during the 2015 reporting year may have been smelted and refined prior to January&nbsp;31, 2013 and are exempt under the Rule because they were outside the supply chain prior to the Rule&#146;s initial reporting period.
While such 3TGs are excluded from the Rule&#146;s scope, our RCOI and supply chain due diligence conducted for the 2015 reporting year may have included such minerals. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">2 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>II.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>REASONABLE COUNTRY OF ORIGIN INQUIRY </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Our RCOI corresponds to the first and second steps of the five-step <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>OECD Due Diligence Guidance for
Responsible Supply Chains of Minerals from Conflict-Affected and High-Risk Areas</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> (&#147;OECD Guidance&#148;), as that Guidance (including its Supplements) applies to each of the 3TGs and to Microsoft as a
&#147;downstream company.&#148; The OECD Guidance provides a framework for detailed due diligence to support responsible global supply chain management of minerals, including 3TGs, and is currently the only nationally or internationally recognized
framework for conflict minerals due diligence. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft does not contract with raw material providers in preparation for manufacturing our
devices and does not source 3TGs directly. We source products from suppliers, which, in turn, source materials, components, and products from their suppliers (&#147;sub-tier suppliers&#148;). Our supply chain is extensive and complex with many
layers of suppliers positioned between ourselves and 3TG SORs. Our contracts require all Microsoft supplier partners to identify, by weight, each and every substance contained in the materials, components, and products supplied to us, including
3TGs. We refer collectively in this CMR to our own manufacturing facilities, contracted manufacturing partners, and our strategic component suppliers as &#147;in-scope suppliers.&#148; Due to our extended supply chain, we leverage our in-scope
suppliers, which provide us with information concerning the sources and chains of custody of 3TGs necessary to the functionality or production of our devices. We provide more detail on our supply chain due diligence process in Section III. The
graphic below demonstrates Microsoft&#146;s span of influence with its suppliers. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g134149stamp_08.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>A.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Establish Strong Company Management Systems </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>1.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Company Policies </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft&#146;s <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Responsible Sourcing of Raw Materials</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">
policy describes our commitment and strategy to responsibly source raw materials used in our devices. Microsoft is committed to the sourcing of raw materials in a way that supports human rights, labor, health and safety, environment, and ethics.
Consistent with this mission, we address the issues associated with the harvesting, extraction, and transportation of raw materials as a global responsibility applicable to all substances used in our devices - unbounded by specific materials or
locations. This policy also states that we implement programs that are region-specific, such as working toward the use of conflict-free minerals in our devices. We expect our suppliers to support our commitment to the responsible sourcing of raw
materials. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">3 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft&#146;s policies also include <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Microsoft&#146;s
Global Human Rights Statement</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">; our </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Supplier Code of Conduct</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">, which defines our expectations concerning
ethical business, employment, environmental, and worker safety practices; and our internal Standards of Business Conduct, which outlines expected behaviors for all Microsoft employees. Microsoft uses supplier specifications and internal procedures
to establish supplier commitments for the responsible sourcing of raw materials, including 3TGs. We incorporate these requirements into our hardware and packaging contracts. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>2.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Internal Management Team </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">A cross-functional team (&#147;team&#148;) supports Microsoft&#146;s responsible sourcing activities, including compliance activities associated with
the Rule. The Corporate Vice President of Microsoft&#146;s Manufacturing and Supply Chain organization is the executive sponsor of the team. Representatives from various Microsoft corporate groups are involved in the development, review and filing
of the CMR. Corporate groups represented on the team include Sourcing, Social and Environmental Accountability, Manufacturing, Accounting/Finance, Internal Audit, Windows and Devices Group, Corporate, External and Legal Affairs, Business and
Corporate Responsibility, Information Services, and Product Environmental Compliance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">This team meets according to Microsoft&#146;s internal
Responsible Sourcing Program Manual and, at a minimum, quarterly to assess the progress of our program and identify steps that are necessary to meet our compliance obligations. The team also trains other internal stakeholders on their roles and
responsibilities for implementing and supporting Microsoft&#146;s responsible sourcing program. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>3.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>System of Supply Chain Controls and Transparency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">We require our in-scope suppliers to fully disclose all substances and materials that are present in the devices or components they supply to us by
component and weight. These material disclosure requirements explicitly cover 3TGs. Our in-scope suppliers are responsible for communicating these 3TG sourcing requirements and specifications to their sub-tier suppliers. Data obtained from our
in-scope suppliers, therefore, includes 3TG information obtained from their sub-tier suppliers. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">In addition, we require all in-scope suppliers to
submit a Conflict Minerals Reporting Template (&#147;CMRT&#148;) annually. These CMRTs are evaluated for completeness, data integrity, due diligence thoroughness, and sourcing risk. Potential risks may include, but are not limited to, failure to
fully complete the CMRT, inconsistencies in the CMRT, and possible sourcing from a Covered Country. If data gaps or risks are identified, Microsoft investigates each issue and engages with those suppliers to address all concerns in conformance to
Microsoft policies, procedures and specifications.. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">In cases where the supplier still poses risk, Microsoft initiates supplier corrective action
calibrated to the severity of the identified risk. H02050 - Microsoft Supplier Social and Environmental Accountability Manual and Microsoft internal operating procedures establish controls for documenting supplier engagement, supplier response, and
corrective action for any non-conformance findings. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">If we confirm that a supplier&#146;s upstream SOR is using raw materials that do not comply
with Microsoft&#146;s Responsible Sourcing of Raw Materials policy or the specifications referenced in this CMR, Microsoft initiates actions to address the non-conformance. These actions may include supplier engagement, training, and/or additional
audits. Microsoft works with impacted suppliers to find alternate sources for non-compliant minerals. If a supplier does not commit to an alternate source within a reasonable time period, Microsoft places the supplier on restricted status with no
new Microsoft business awarded until any non-conformance is resolved. Termination of Microsoft&#146;s business relationship with the supplier may also occur. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">4 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft is a longstanding member of the <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Global
e-Sustainability Initiative</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> (&#147;GeSI&#148;) and the </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Electronics Industry Citizenship Coalition</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">
(&#147;EICC&#148;) - two organizations that initiated the </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Conflict-Free Sourcing Initiative</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> (&#147;CFSI&#148;). Founded in 2008 by GeSI and EICC
members, the CFSI is one of the most utilized and respected resources for addressing supply chain conflict minerals issues. The CFSI, through its CFSP, uses an independent third-party audit to verify SORs that demonstrate that the 3TGs, which they
process, do not originate from sources that may be directly or indirectly financing or benefitting armed groups in a Covered Country. Microsoft funded an early adopters program that provided initial audit funds, enabling more SORs to be CFSP
audited. Microsoft also provides financial support to the </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Industrial Technology Research Institute&#146;s Tin Supply Chain Initiative</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">
(&#147;iTSCi&#148;) that has established a system of traceability and due diligence in Covered Countries and we support the efforts of organizations, including the </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Public-Private Alliance for
Minerals Trade</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> (&#147;PPA&#148;), that promote responsible mining and raw material sourcing. Microsoft is a sponsor of the </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Multi-Stakeholder
Group</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">, hosted by the </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Responsible Sourcing Network</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">, which coordinates efforts to promote security and
stability in the DRC region by engaging governments to bring an end to the conflict in the DRC. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft works to positively impact
end-to-end mining sustainability, from artisanal mines to larger mining enterprises. Through this work, we aspire to improve conditions directly at the source across a broad scope of issues in partnership with the electronics industry, the mining
industry, and other not-for-profit partners. In particular, Microsoft believes that it can improve practices associated with the mining of metal ores at their source through participation in collaborative initiatives related to the upstream mining
industry. Microsoft supports and participates in numerous additional partnerships that work to establish responsible mining standards and the responsible sourcing of minerals, including the following: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><FONT COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Initiative for Responsible Mining Assurance (&#147;IRMA&#148;)</U></FONT>: established a
multi-stakeholder and independently verifiable responsible mining assurance system that improves social and environmental performance; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><FONT COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Pact</U></FONT>: empowers small and medium sized miners to achieve legal, safe and secure
livelihoods; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><FONT COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Alliance for Responsible Mining (&#147;ARM&#148;)</U></FONT>: sets standards for responsible
artisanal and small scale mining and supports and creates opportunities for gold miners and provides them incentives to become responsible economic, technological and environmental enterprises. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&nbsp;&nbsp;4.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>&nbsp;&nbsp;Supplier Engagement </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">In light of our corporate size, the complexity of our devices, and the depth, breadth, and constant evolution of our supply chain; we rely on our
in-scope suppliers to provide us with information concerning the source and chain of custody of 3TGs contained in the products and components they supply to us. Many of our in-scope suppliers are also subject to the Rule, and they rely on
information provided by their upstream suppliers to meet their compliance obligations. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">5 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">We drive responsible sourcing through our extended supply chain by surveying our in-scope suppliers&#146;
sourcing of raw materials in their upstream supply chains. We also use tools that include supplier and smelter capability building and support broader industry efforts to promote responsible mining and sourcing. Finally, we conduct audits of our
contracted suppliers to verify conformance to Microsoft requirements. More information is set forth below. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><U>Supplier Requirements</U>: We require our in-scope suppliers to meet our material disclosure requirements and related
responsible sourcing policies through contractual provisions and product specifications that we communicate, monitor, and track electronically to ensure conformance. These policies and procedures are outlined in Section III. We also train our
directly contracted suppliers to meet our requirements through training sessions, educational forums, and direct communications. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><U>Capability Building and Partnerships</U>: We work closely with our supply chain partners to build the raw material
supplier capabilities for achieving our responsible sourcing goals. We invest in industry programs, such as the CFSP, to increase suppliers&#146; capabilities and provide them with platforms to share best practices with each other.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><U>Supplier Audits</U>: Microsoft conducts audits of its contracted suppliers to assess their conformance to Microsoft
requirements, including supply chain transparency. All new contracted hardware and packaging suppliers undergo an initial capability assessment to verify conformance to Microsoft requirements. Microsoft requires that suppliers have a policy and
effective procedures to establish and monitor their responsible sourcing of raw materials. Microsoft selects and retains only those business partners that commit to meeting these requirements. A failure by a supplier or any sub-tier supplier to
conform to these requirements may constitute a breach of the supplier&#146;s contractual agreement with Microsoft. During the 2015 reporting year, Microsoft-engaged auditors conducted onsite audits of 129 contracted hardware and packaging suppliers
to assess areas of SEA conformance, including whether the suppliers had an established conflict minerals policy, systems in place to implement that policy, and documentation to verify conformance to Microsoft responsible sourcing requirements.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">CFSI&#146;s &#147;<FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Practical Guidance for Downstream Companies</U></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">&#148; document states that &#147;all of the [OECD Guidance&#146;s] red flag triggers are contained in the upstream portion of the supply chain.&#148; Because these conflict mineral supply chain &#147;triggers&#148; are
directed to upstream companies, rather than downstream manufacturers, such as Microsoft, we mitigate risks associated with the sourcing of 3TGs by working with our in-scope suppliers to identify 3TG SORs and encourage those facilities to become CFSP
compliant or, failing to do so, use an alternate facility that is CFSP compliant. We also participate in industry-wide initiatives, such as the CFSP, that assess SOR compliance with the OECD Guidance as recommended by CFSI guidance documents. We
require our in-scope suppliers to actively work with their upstream suppliers to mitigate risks associated with their sourcing of 3TGs. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">6 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>5.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Grievance Mechanism </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Microsoft&#146;s Global Human Rights Statement</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> expresses
our commitment to provide an anonymous grievance reporting mechanism for our employees and other stakeholders who may be impacted by our operations. Microsoft&#146;s </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Business Conduct
Hotline</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> provides that mechanism, which allows employees and others to ask compliance questions or report concerns regarding Microsoft&#146;s business operations, including its mineral sourcing policies or
those of its suppliers. We investigate and, where appropriate, take remedial action to address reported incidents. We also participate in industry efforts to develop specific grievance mechanisms for conflict minerals-related issues, including
PPA&#146;s efforts to establish an in-region hotline. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>B.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Identify and Assess Risk in the Supply Chain </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">We took the following steps to identify and assess supplier conflict mineral sourcing risk in connection with 2015 reporting year data<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Using the Rule and SEC guidance, we generated a list of potential in-scope suppliers to receive Microsoft&#146;s annual
CMRT survey. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">We surveyed all potential in-scope suppliers to determine the status of any 3TGs contained in devices manufactured
during the 2015 reporting year by utilizing the CFSI-standard CMRT and the services of a third party solution provider. The survey included questions regarding a supplier&#146;s responsible sourcing policies, its practices for engaging with its
upstream suppliers, a request to list all SORs from which its 3TGs were sourced, and other detailed questions concerning the origins of 3TGs contained in the supplier&#146;s products as well as its 3TG due diligence policies and procedures.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">The survey followed the OECD Guidance as tailored for Microsoft&#146;s role as a downstream company. We reviewed all
supplier CMRT submissions to validate that they were complete and to identify any contradictions or inconsistencies. We worked with our third-party solution provider to secure updated responses from suppliers, as needed. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">We identified 276 active and in-scope suppliers for reporting year 2015. Of the 276 active and in-scope suppliers
surveyed, we received responses from 267. This resulted in a 97% response rate - an improvement from the 2014 reporting year rate of 82% and the 2013 reporting year rate of 71% as shown in Figure 1. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:26%">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> Microsoft completed its supplier conflict mineral sourcing data analysis for the 2015 reporting year on March&nbsp;31, 2016. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">7 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Figure 1. Response Rate for Active and In-scope Suppliers (2013-2015 Reporting Years) </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g134149stamp_13.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>III. DUE DILIGENCE DESIGN AND PERFORMANCE </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">On the basis of our RCOI, we determined that 3TGs contained in our devices may have originated in one or more Covered Country. Accordingly, we designed
and performed due diligence on the source and chain-of-custody of those 3TGs. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>A.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Due Diligence Design </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Our 3TG due diligence process conforms to the third and fourth steps of the five-step OECD Guidance. The first and second steps of the five-step OECD
Guidance were addressed in Section II. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>B.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Due Diligence Performed </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>1.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Design and Implement a Strategy to Respond to Risks </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft requires its suppliers to take affirmative actions to minimize the possible sourcing of 3TGs from conflict-affected and high-risk areas. This
is required through contracts with our suppliers and supplier specifications. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="9%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>a.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Microsoft Supplier Specifications - H00594 and HO0642 </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft&#146;s supplier specification H00594, Restricted Substances for Hardware Products (&#147;H00594&#148;), requires 100 percent identification of
all materials, including 3TG, used in all packaging and hardware products and parts supplied to Microsoft on a component-by-component level. Specifically, H00594 requires contracted suppliers to do the following: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Post a responsible sourcing policy, conforming to the OECD Guidance, on their website; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">8 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Exercise due diligence on the source and chain of custody of any 3TG contained in materials, components, or products
they supply to Microsoft; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Identify, by name, each SOR that has processed or otherwise handled 3TGs contained in those materials, components, or
products; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Encourage those SORs to participate in the CFSP or an equivalent third-party conflict-free audit scheme, when available;
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Confirm that 3TGs in their supply chain are sourced from SORs that are compliant with the CFSP or an equivalent
independent private sector audit firm, when available; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Notify Microsoft immediately if they obtain information or knowledge that the minerals used in the materials,
components, or products that they supply to Microsoft may contain 3TGs sourced from a Covered Country. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">H00594 requires Microsoft
suppliers to impose these same requirements on their sub-tier suppliers and to provide appropriate training and support to help their sub-tier suppliers meet Microsoft responsible sourcing requirements. To facilitate this process, H00642, Restricted
Substances Control System for Hardware Products. requires Microsoft suppliers to utilize the common CMRT provided by the CFSI and found at <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>www.conflictfreesourcing.org</U></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">. Suppliers are responsible for submitting the annual CMRT as well as updating the CMRT upon request or when changes occur. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="9%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>b.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Responsible Sourcing Program Manual Processes to Implement OECD Guidance </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">To respond to possible conflict mineral risks that were identified during our due diligence process, Microsoft implemented responsible sourcing
practices, to communicate with suppliers that may be sourcing 3TGs under conditions that may be directly or indirectly financing or benefitting armed groups in a Covered Country. Under our Responsible Sourcing of Raw Materials Program, we use the
OECD Guidance to review supplier CMRT data and identify potential red flags for the sourcing of 3TGs, including the following: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">The minerals originated from or were transported via a conflict-affected or high-risk area; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">The minerals were claimed to originate from a country that has limited known reserves for the mineral in question;
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">The minerals were claimed to originate from a country in which minerals from conflict-affected and high-risk areas are
known to transit; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">The company&#146;s suppliers or other known upstream companies have shareholder or other interests in companies that
supply minerals or operate in one of the red flag locations of mineral origin and transit; and </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">The company&#146;s suppliers&#146; or other known upstream companies were known to have sourced minerals from a red flag
location of mineral origin and transit in the last 12 months. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">9 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft&#146;s program includes an escalation process that may require an in-scope supplier to find an
alternative to a non-CFSP compliant source of 3TGs for use in materials, components, or products supplied to Microsoft or risk termination as a Microsoft supplier. To date, we have not encountered a responsible sourcing issue with a supplier that
has warranted contract termination. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Also, as required by Microsoft&#146;s internal Responsible Sourcing Program Manual, our team assessed the
progress of our conflict minerals program and identified steps necessary to meet our compliance obligations. The team also provided monthly program status updates, including metrics and audit results, to Microsoft&#146;s Corporate Vice President of
Manufacturing and Supply Chain organization. We utilized supplier survey updates, supplier communications, supplier social and environmental accountability audits, and new supplier briefings to prevent the introduction of any new 3TG sourcing risk
to our supply chain. We also leveraged meetings with executives to report findings and receive program guidance. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="9%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>c.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Industry and NGO Partner Engagement </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft participated in, or has been a member of, several industry-wide responsible mining and smelting initiatives, including CFSI, PPA, ITRI&#146;s
iTSCi program, IRMA, Pact, and ARM. As part of our due diligence, we also conducted smelter outreach on behalf of the CFSI Smelter Engagement Team. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>2.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Carried Out Independent Third-Party Audit of Supply Chain Due Diligence </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">As contemplated by the OECD Guidance, our due diligence program leveraged independent SOR audits, which were undertaken in accordance with the CFSP and
other similar programs. Microsoft obtained SOR data from the CFSP Compliant Smelter List through our membership in the CFSI using the <I>Reasonable Country of Origin Inquiry Data</I> for member <I>MSFT</I>. This data was used to support certain
statements contained in this CMR. The CFSP Compliant Smelter List is a published list of SORs that have undergone assessment through the CFSP or industry equivalent program (such as Responsible Jewellery Council or London Bullion Market Association
(&#147;LBMA&#148;)). Microsoft also participated in CFSI&#146;s Smelter Engagement Team during the 2015 reporting year and we engaged a third party to assist smelters prepare for CFSP audits. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>3.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Reported on Supply Chain Due Diligence </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft&#146;s <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Responsible Sourcing of Raw Materials</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">
policy and other responsible sourcing documents are available on our external website. We have filed our CMR, required by the Rule, with the SEC and we have posted it on our external
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0563c1"><U>Responsible Sourcing</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> website. These disclosures meet the fifth step of the five-step OECD Guidance. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">10 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>IV.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>SOR INFORMATION </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>A.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>3TG Processing Facilities </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft has made a reasonable good faith effort to collect and evaluate information concerning 3TG SORs based on data provided by our in-scope
suppliers. The vast majority of our in-scope suppliers provided data at a company or divisional level or otherwise were unable to identify specific entities that had processed 3TGs contained in the materials, components, or products supplied to us.
This was expected given the multiple tiers of supply chain actors that are positioned between our in-scope suppliers and 3TG SORs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Our supplier
survey data revealed 19,568 potential 3TG SORs in the Microsoft supply chain. We validated the data by removing duplicate SORs, reconciling multiple SOR names for a single entity, and eliminating otherwise invalid SOR names. This process reduced the
list to 688 entities. Of this list, 226 SORs were unknown to CFSI (but are being investigated by CFSI members) and another 160 SORs were confirmed as misidentified and/or were not actual SORs. After removing those entities, 302 SORs remained. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Figures below provide a visual depiction of the SORs identified in Microsoft&#146;s supply chain by CFSP audit status. Figure 2 categorizes the SORs
by audit status and reporting year. Figure 3 categorizes the SORs by 3TG mineral and audit status. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Appendix A to this CMR lists the 302 SORs which,
to the extent known, processed 3TGs in Microsoft devices during the 2015 reporting year. Appendix A provides each SOR&#146;s country location, 3TG processed, and CFSP audit status. Appendix A includes several gold SORs which have received the LBMA
Responsible Gold Certificate - these are marked with an asterisk. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Table 1 (below) summarizes the conflict mineral status of the 302 SORs that were
identified in the Microsoft supply chain. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">CFSI defines each audit stage in the following manner: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Countries of origin for the 3TGs that were identified by our CFSP-compliant SORs include: Argentina, Angola, Australia, Austria, Belgium, Brazil,
Burundi, Cambodia, Canada, Central African Republic, Chile, China, Colombia, C&ocirc;te D&#146;Ivoire, Czech Republic, Djibouti, Ecuador, Egypt, Estonia, Ethiopia, France, Germany, Guyana, Hungary, India, Indonesia, Ireland, Israel, Japan,
Kazakhstan, Kenya, Laos, Luxembourg, Madagascar, Malaysia, Mongolia, Mozambique, Myanmar, Namibia, Netherlands, Nigeria, Peru, Portugal, Republic of Congo, Russia, Rwanda, Sierra Leone, Singapore, Slovakia, South Africa, South Korea, South Sudan,
Spain, Suriname, Switzerland, Taiwan, Tanzania, Thailand, Uganda, United Kingdom, United States of America, Vietnam, Zambia, and Zimbabwe. Other countries of origin identified through additional due diligence included: Armenia, Belarus, Ghana,
Guinea, Hong Kong, Italy, Jersey, Kyrgyzstan, Mali, Mexico, Morocco, Niger, Papua New Guinea, Philippines, Poland, Saudi Arabia, Sweden, Tajikistan, Turkey, United Arab Emirates, and Uzbekistan. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Figure 8 provides a graphical presentation of the countries of origin for 3TGs that were identified as being used in the Microsoft supply chain during
the 2015 reporting year. Although Covered Countries are listed in Microsoft&#146;s countries of origin list, the SORs located in those countries are CFSP-compliant, verifying that they have been determined by CFSP to source 3TGs in a manner that
does not directly or indirectly finance or benefit armed groups in a Covered Country. At this time, we have country-of-origin information for CFSP-compliant SORs and countries identified through additional due diligence. </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>3TG Mines or Locations of Origin </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft obtained Reasonable Country of Origin data through our membership in the CFSI using the <I>Reasonable Country of Origin Inquiry Data</I> for
member <I>MSFT</I>. We used this data to determine the 3TG country of origin of SORs identified in Microsoft&#146;s supply chain. Microsoft supports the continued refinement and expansion of the list of participating SORs in the CFSP audit program
through our membership in CFSI, which oversees the CFSP. We encourage SORs to participate in the CFSP by contacting all non-compliant SORs identified in our supply chain each reporting year. We also require all of our suppliers that reported
non-compliant SORs to conduct outreach to those SORs and encourage them to join the CFSP. In addition, we have encouraged other SORs to participate in the CFSP by contacting SORs directly and by engaging in outreach events to encourage greater CFSP
participation. We funded a third party to help educate SORs and prepare the SORs for the audit process. We have also offered to visit SORs to facilitate their participation in the CFSP. </P>
<P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:26%">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify"><SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP> These numbers include metrics on indirect sourcing that were not included in the 2014 reporting year report as they were made available for the first time this year by CFSI. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">17 </P>

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>V.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>IMPROVEMENTS </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft&#146;s key 2015 reporting year accomplishments and improvements are detailed below. Although comparisons to the 2014 reporting year data are
of limited utility due to supply chain year-to-year variances in the data pool, this year&#146;s report, which documents our efforts to expand the number of verified conflict-free SORs in our supply chain, demonstrates meaningful progress, including
the following improvements: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

supplier outreach, and maturation of CFSI&#146;s CFSP; </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>VI.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>FUTURE ACTIONS </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft is committed to the sourcing of raw materials in ways that fundamentally support human rights, labor, health and safety, environmental
protection, and business ethics in our supply chain. We will continue to improve our ability to identify, assess, and mitigate risks associated with our raw materials sourcing. We will continue to implement our Responsible Sourcing of Raw Materials
policy that includes a combination of building cross-industry sector capability, supporting electronics industry efforts, implementing region-specific programs such as working toward the use of conflict-free minerals in our devices and working with
in-region expert NGOs that are able to implement community programs that are linguistically and culturally effective. Encouraging SORs to participate in the CFSP will improve our knowledge about the 3TGs in our raw material supply chain and we will
continue to encourage CFSP participation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Microsoft is aware of concerns that have been raised regarding the Rule&#146;s possible unintended
negative consequences for local communities. Microsoft is committed to complying with the OECD Guidance and the Rule in such a way that mitigates such concerns through implementation of our Responsible Sourcing of Raw Materials program, which is a
holistic program that extends beyond the geographic limitations and the scope of the Rule.&nbsp;Consistent with our commitments, we intend to take the following steps to continuously improve our responsible sourcing of raw materials due diligence
efforts:</P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt ;font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Continue to refine and improve internal procedures and processes to enhance alignment with the OECD Guidance, including
Microsoft&#146;s supplier escalation process and supplier audit procedures; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
